################################################################################
#
# PRAAT COMPLETE CAPABILITY CATALOGUE
# ====================================
# Source: github.com/praat/praat.github.io (cloned and parsed)
# Version: 6.4.62 (March 13, 2026)
# Extraction date: 2026-03-20
# Method: Automated extraction from C++ source via git clone + Python parsing
#
# To the extent possible under the Praat license, this document is Part of EML 
# PraatGen GPL-3.0-or-later — Ian Howell, Embodied Music Lab
#
# This is the definitive reference of everything Praat can do, extracted
# directly from the source code. It serves as a fallback/supplement to the
# COMMANDS_*.txt files in the EML Praat Assistant Project Knowledge.
#
# CONTENTS:
#   §1  Class hierarchy (object inheritance)
#   §2  All commands with parameters and defaults (2,089 single-class,
#       360 cross-class, 318 menu — 1,538 with full parameter defaults)
#   §3  Formula engine: all 336 built-in functions with signatures
#   §4  Scripting engine capabilities
#   §5  Capabilities for the "Praat is more than you think" paper
#
# COVERAGE NOTES:
#   - ~32 KlattGrid commands from C-preprocessor macro expansion are not
#     captured (compile-time string concatenation: ##Name##)
#   - FORM_READ/FORM_SAVE blocks (108 total, mostly file I/O dialogs)
#     are captured as commands but without parameter detail
#   - DO_ALTERNATIVE patterns (21 total) may show as duplicates with
#     old/new parameter sets — the later (more params) is current
#
################################################################################


################################################################################
# §1 CLASS HIERARCHY
# Key object types and their inheritance chains.
# Critical insight: Sound IS a Matrix, so Formula: operates on it at C speed.
################################################################################

# Core analysis chain
Sound -> Vector -> Matrix -> SampledXY -> Sampled -> Function -> Daata -> Thing
LongSound -> SampledXY (direct file-backed, not Matrix)
Pitch -> Sampled -> Function
Formant -> Sampled -> Function
Intensity -> Vector -> Matrix
Spectrum -> Matrix
Spectrogram -> Matrix
Harmonicity -> Vector -> Matrix
PointProcess -> Function
TextGrid -> Function
Table -> Daata (NOT Matrix — row/column, not sampled)
TableOfReal -> Daata

# Spectral/cepstral
PowerCepstrogram -> Matrix
PowerCepstrum -> Cepstrum -> Matrix
Ltas -> Vector -> Matrix
Cochleagram -> Matrix

# Tiers (all inherit time-point structure)
PitchTier -> RealTier -> AnyTier -> Function
IntensityTier -> RealTier
DurationTier -> RealTier
AmplitudeTier -> RealTier
FormantGrid -> Function (contains multiple RealTier tracks)

# Synthesis
Manipulation -> Function (contains PitchTier + DurationTier + Sound)
KlattGrid -> Function

# Statistics (David Weenink)
PCA -> Eigen -> Daata
Discriminant -> Daata
Configuration -> TableOfReal
Dissimilarity -> Proximity -> TableOfReal
MixingMatrix -> TableOfReal

# Special
Electroglottogram -> Sound -> Vector -> Matrix
PatternList -> Matrix (neural net input)
ActivationList -> Matrix (neural net output)
DTW -> Matrix


################################################################################
# §2 ALL COMMANDS WITH PARAMETERS AND DEFAULTS
################################################################################

Cross-class commands: 360 (179 with parameters)
Menu commands: 318 (157 with parameters)
FORM blocks parsed: 1749
================================================================================

  Formula...
    # for col := 1 to ncol do { self [row, col] := `formula' ; x := x + dx } y := y + dy }}
    FORMULA        Formula = "self"

  To Matrix

  To PatternList

  Formula...
    # # ncol = the number of points
    # for col from 1 to ncol
    #    # x = the time of the colth point, in seconds
    #    # self = the value of the colth point, in Pascal
    #    self = `formula'
    # endfor
    FORMULA        Formula = "- self ; upside down"

################################################################################
# §3 FORMULA ENGINE — ALL 336 BUILT-IN FUNCTIONS
#
# Available in ANY Formula: command, script-level expressions, and
# beginPause/form field defaults.
#
# The Formula engine operates at C speed. When applied to a Matrix-derived
# object (Sound, Spectrum, Spectrogram, Intensity, Harmonicity, etc.),
# it iterates all cells automatically — no Praat-level loop needed.
#
# Key: Formula + object[] cross-referencing ≈ NumPy vectorization.
# Source: fon/manual_functions.cpp (178 KB), sys/Formula.cpp (374 KB)
################################################################################

abs (%`x`) – absolute value
abs# (%`vector#`) – absolute value of each element of %`vector#`
abs## (%`matrix##`) – absolute value of each cell of %`matrix##`
appDay ( ) – the month day at which the present version of Praat was built
appendFile (%`filePath$`, `...`) – write texts, numbers, vectors and so on
appendFileLine (%`filePath$`, `...`) – write texts, numbers, vectors and so on,
appendInfo (`...`) – write texts, numbers, vectors and so on,
appendInfoLine (`...`) – write texts, numbers, vectors and so on,
appMonth ( ) – the month in which the present version of Praat was built (between 1 and 12)
appMonth$ ( ) – the name of the month (in English) in which the present version of Praat was built
appVersion ( ) – the number of the present version of Praat
appVersion$ ( ) – the present version of Praat, as text
appYear ( ) – the year in which the present version of Praat was built
arccos (%`x`) – inverse cosine
arccos# (%`vector#`) – inverse cosine of each element of %`vector#`
arccos## (%`matrix##`) – inverse cosine of each cell of %`matrix##`
arccosh (%`x`) – inverse hyperbolic cosine
arccosh# (%`vector#`) – inverse hyperbolic cosine of each element of %`vector#`
arccosh## (%`matrix##`) – inverse hyperbolic cosine of each cell of %`matrix##`
arcsin (%`x`) – inverse sine
arcsin# (%`vector#`) – inverse sine of each element of %`vector#`
arcsin## (%`matrix##`) – inverse sine of each cell of %`matrix##`
arcsinh (%`x`) – inverse hyperbolic sine
arcsinh# (%`vector#`) – inverse hyperbolic sine of each element of %`vector#`
arcsinh## (%`matrix##`) – inverse hyperbolic sine of each cell of %`matrix##`
arctan (%`x`) – inverse tangent
arctan# (%`vector#`) – inverse tangent of each element of %`vector#`
arctan## (%`matrix##`) – inverse tangent of each cell of %`matrix##`
arctan2 (%`y`, %`x`) – argument angle
arctanh (%`x`) – inverse hyperbolic tangent
arctanh# (%`vector#`) – inverse hyperbolic tangent of each element of %`vector#`
arctanh## (%`matrix##`) – inverse hyperbolic tangent of each cell of %`matrix##`
assert %`condition` – condition checking
asserterror %`message$` – testing that a certain error occurs
asynchronous – let the script continue while the sound is playing or a subprocess is running
backslashTrigraphsToUnicode$ (%`string$`) – convert e.g. \bsct to \ct
barkToHertz (%`x`) – from Bark-rate to acoustic frequency
besselI (%`n`, %`x`) – modified Bessel function of the first kind, %I__%n_
besselK (%`n`, %`x`) – modified Bessel function of the second kind, %K__%n_
beta (%`x`, %`y`) – \be function

################################################################################
# §4 SCRIPTING ENGINE CAPABILITIES
# Source: sys/Interpreter.cpp (156 KB), sys/Formula.cpp (374 KB)
################################################################################

CONTROL FLOW:
  if / elsif / elif / else / endif / fi
  for / from / to / endfor
  while / endwhile
  repeat / until
  goto / label
  procedure: name / endproc
  
VARIABLE TYPES:
  Numeric:      x = 42
  String:       x$ = "hello"
  Vector:       x# = { 1, 2, 3 }    or   x# = zero# (100)
  Matrix:       x## = zero## (10, 20)
  String array: x$# = { "a", "b", "c" }

INDEXED VARIABLES:
  x[i]      — numeric array (main body)
  x$[i]     — string array (main body)
  x#[i]     — vector element
  x##[i,j]  — matrix element
  .x[.i]    — numeric array (procedure scope)
  .x$[.i]   — string array (procedure scope)

PROCEDURES:
  procedure myProc: .arg1, .arg2$
    .localVar = .arg1 * 2
    .result$ = .arg2$ + " processed"
  endproc
  @myProc: 42, "hello"
  result = myProc.localVar
  # All local variables prefixed with .
  # Accessible after call via procedureName.varName

I/O COMMANDS:
  writeInfoLine: / appendInfoLine: / writeInfo: / appendInfo:
  writeFile: / writeFileLine: / appendFile: / appendFileLine:
  readFile() / readFile$() / readFile#() / readFile##()
  readLinesFromFile$#()

GUI (User Input):
  form: / endform          — one per script, at top only
  beginPause: / endPause:  — anywhere, multiple allowed
  pauseScript:             — modal message, OK only
  chooseReadFile$: / chooseWriteFile$: / chooseFolder$:
  
  Form field types: real, positive, integer, natural, word, sentence,
  text, boolean, choice, optionmenu, option, comment, infile, outfile,
  folder, realvector, positivevector, integervector, naturalvector

DEMO WINDOW (interactive graphics application framework):
  demoShow / demoWaitForInput / demoPeekInput
  demoClicked / demoClickedIn / demoX / demoY
  demoKeyPressed / demoKey$ / demoInput
  demoShiftKeyPressed / demoCommandKeyPressed / demoOptionKeyPressed
  demoWindowTitle

SYSTEM INTERACTION:
  runScript / runSystem / runSystem$ / runSubprocess / runSubprocess$
  stopwatch / clock / sleep
  environment$
  asynchronous (modifier — run subprocess without blocking)
  fileNames$# / folderNames$# — directory listing with glob patterns
  fileReadable / folderExists / createFolder / deleteFile
  moveAndOrRenameFile

OBJECT MANAGEMENT:
  selectObject: / plusObject: / minusObject: / removeObject:
  selected() / selected$() / numberOfSelected() / selected#() / selected$#()
  editor / endeditor — enter/leave editor scripting environment

ASSERTIONS:
  assert <condition>
  asserterror <expected_message>

SPECIAL MODIFIERS:
  nocheck — suppress error on next command
  nowarn — suppress warning on next command  
  noprogress — suppress progress bar on next command

REGULAR EXPRESSIONS:
  Full POSIX regex via index_regex(), rindex_regex(), replace_regex$()
  Engine: melder/regularExp.cpp (123 KB)

MATRIX/VECTOR OPERATIONS (all C-speed in Formula engine):
  Arithmetic:   +, -, *, /  (element-wise on vectors/matrices)
  Creation:     zero#(n), zero##(r,c), linear#, to#, from_to#, from_to_by#
  Random:       randomUniform#, randomGauss#, randomInteger#, etc.
  Linear alg:   inner, outer##, mul##, mul_tn##, solve#, solve##, transpose##
  Aggregation:  sum, mean, stdev, center, min, max, imin, imax, quantile, norm
  Sorting:      sort#, shuffle#, sort$#, sort_numberAware$#
  Statistics:   correlation, rowSums#, columnSums#
  ML:           sigmoid#, softmax#, softmaxPerRow##, rectify#




################################################################################
# §5 CAPABILITIES FOR "PRAAT IS MORE THAN YOU THINK" PAPER
################################################################################

COMPUTATIONAL ENGINE:
  Formula: engine operates at C speed on all Matrix-derived objects
  (Sound, Spectrum, Spectrogram, Intensity, Harmonicity, etc.)
  Cross-object referencing: object[id] and object["name"] in formulas
  → Functionally equivalent to NumPy vectorization for element-wise ops
  Source: sys/Formula.cpp (374 KB)

STATISTICS (built-in functions, no packages needed):
  Distribution functions: chiSquareP/Q, studentP/Q, fisherP/Q,
    binomialP/Q, gaussP/Q, incompleteBeta, incompleteGammaP
  Inverse functions: invChiSquareQ, invStudentQ, invFisherQ,
    invGaussQ, invBinomialP/Q
  Special functions: erf, erfc, lnGamma, beta, lnBeta, besselI, besselK
  Table object: grouping, formula-based computation, statistical queries

LINEAR ALGEBRA (native, no external libraries):
  solve# (Ax=b), solve## (AX=B)
  solveWeaklyConstrained#, solveNonnegative#, solveSparse#
  mul##, mul_tn##, mul_nt##, mul_tt## — matrix multiplication variants
  transpose##, inner, outer##, correlation
  Eigen decomposition (native object: Eigen → PCA, Discriminant)
  SVD (native object type)
  Source: dwsys/NUM2.cpp (93 KB)

MACHINE LEARNING (native implementations):
  FFNet — feed-forward neural networks (backpropagation training)
  GaussianMixture — GMM fitting via EM algorithm
  HMM — Hidden Markov Models (Baum-Welch, Viterbi)
  Discriminant analysis (linear and quadratic)
  PCA — dimensionality reduction
  NMF — non-negative matrix factorization
  sigmoid/softmax activation in Formula engine

SIGNAL PROCESSING:
  FFT (Sound ↔ Spectrum, bidirectional)
  Autocorrelation, cross-correlation, convolution
  Filtering: pass/stop Hann band, pre/de-emphasis, formula-based
  Resampling (multiple interpolation methods incl. sinc70)
  LPC analysis and resynthesis (Burg, autocorrelation, covariance, Marple)
  Cepstral analysis (PowerCepstrogram, CPPS)
  Hilbert transform (via AnalyticSound)

MULTIDIMENSIONAL SCALING:
  Dissimilarity → Configuration via SMACOF, Kruskal, etc.
  Procrustes rotation, individual differences MDS
  Distance matrices with multiple metrics

  Full POSIX regex in index_regex, rindex_regex, replace_regex$
